The process involves coating a glass plate with chemicals and exposing it to light through the camera. A fixative is then applied to stop the process and set the picture. The process must be started and finished within 15 minutes, and the camera's shutter has to remain open for longer in low light conditions, resulting in exposures of up to 12 seconds.  ## Analysis of Response B  The Victorian photographic method used by Jack Lowe involves coating a glass plate with chemicals and exposing it to light. This produces an image known as an ambrotype. The fixative then sets the picture. With exposures of up to 12 seconds, the subject must be willing to participate. The process is started and finished in about 15 minutes.  ## Reason of A=B  Both responses accurately describe the Victorian photographic method used by Jack Lowe and the process he uses to capture the RNLI volunteers.
